From a multiple page menu, it seemed that only a few items were actually available. Luckily, our driver, Vincent, who helped us get around the resort came to the rescue and came up with a plan. He then helped us to pre-order our dinners each night to guarantee the food we wanted would be ready on our arrival. We also want to mention that once we arrived at the restaurant each night, our waitress, Laura, provided us with amazing service. She was always friendly and attended to our needs with a smile. 

We are looking forward to visiting again in the future.

msg:Lushan Xihai is a national 5A scenic spot that has been featured in "Aerial Photography of China". It is actually an hour and a half drive from Lushan. After coming down from Lushan, I looked for a hotel in Lushan Xihai. The only luxury hotel was this Hilton Curio Collection, so I navigated all the way there. Only when we arrived did we find out that the hotel is located to the northwest of the West Sea, and Sima Wharf, the main scenic spot of the West Sea in Lushan, is to the southeast. The difference is more than 40 kilometers and 50 minutes' drive.
But everything is the best arrangement. This hotel is the destination and should be a representative of Jiangxi luxury hotels. The island covers an area of ‚Äã‚Äã150,000 square meters, with a construction area of ‚Äã‚Äãonly 50,000 square meters. More than 100 staff serve more than 100 rooms. Almost all of them are villa rooms, and the service is particularly attentive.
I slept very well in the hotel and participated in the "Island Owner Tour" specially organized by the hotel the next morning. The hotel manager, Mr. Zhu, personally led a small group of guests to tour and introduce the entire hotel. From the art center that won the international architectural award to the Daze Pavilion facing the West Sea with lakes and mountains like a splash-ink painting. Mr. Zhu introduced the history, geography, vegetation and food of Xihai and the hotel, and gave everyone a glimpse into a certain period of development history, leaving deep memories.
I would also like to give special praise to Manager Lu of the concierge depar**ent. His service is meticulous, well-coordinated and very professional.
Finally, it is recommended that the hotel improve the quality of breakfast. The variety does not need to be rich, but the quality of the individual items should be more refined, so as to be worthy of the hotel's positioning.
